 	function CheckForm1(f) {
 		var email_re = /[a-z0-9!#$%&'*+\/=?^_`{|}~-]+(?:\.[a-z0-9!#$%&'*+\/=?^_`{|}~-]+)*@(?:[a-z0-9](?:[a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?\.)+[a-z0-9](?:[a-z0-9-]*[a-z0-9])?/i;
 		if (!email_re.test(f.email.value)) {
 			alert("Пожалуйста, введите ваш e-mail");
 			f.email.focus();
 			return false;
 		}
 		window.open('', 'letter', 'width=723,height=469,status=no,resizable=no,scrollbars=no');
 	}
 	function hideDefault(field) {
 		var form = field.parentNode;
 		form.temp_val.value = field.value;
 		field.value = '';
 		field.removeEventListener('focus', hideDefault, false);
 		field.addEventListener('blur', checkForEmpty, false);
 	}
 	function checkForEmpty(field) {
 		if (field.value.length == 0) {
 			var form = field.parentNode;
 			field.value = form.temp_val.value;
 			field.addEventListener('focus', hideDefault, false);
 			field.removeEventListener('blur', checkForEmpty, false);
 		}
 	}

 	function hideDefault(field) {
 		var form = field.parentNode;
 		form.temp_val.value = field.value;
 		field.value = '';
 		field.removeEventListener('focus', hideDefault, false);
 		field.addEventListener('blur', checkForEmpty, false);
 	}
 	function checkForEmpty(field) {
 		if (field.value.length == 0) {
 			var form = field.parentNode;
 			field.value = form.temp_val.value;
 			field.addEventListener('focus', hideDefault, false);
 			field.removeEventListener('blur', checkForEmpty, false);
 		}
 	}
